BUSTY FANTASY BURST - COMPLETE CHARACTER STATS WITH LEVEL BREAKDOWN
R: 18 | SR: 29 | SSR: 51 | Total: 98
============================================================================================================================================

PROGRESSION SYSTEMS:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
• LIMIT BREAK (LB1-LB5): Each level adds permanent stat bonuses
• GP ABILITY / BOND (Lv1-10): Shows per-level stat gains
• ABILITY GRADE (Grade 1-10): Each grade adds bonus when Passive Ability 5 unlocked
• 5 PASSIVE ABILITIES: 5 abilities per grade, values increase at each grade (Grade 1-10)

CRITICAL SYSTEM: Crit Rate % = Crit Value / 20
